The rear airflow is a much better solution to avoid breakage, but needs to have hotter temperatures to actually straighten the hair. My hair is EXTREMELY curly and I have tried most every hair dryer out there to blow it straight. This new product falls very short of my expectations, however, is on the right track for the perfect styler-dryer.
